 com / 5bocqiijha — ANI (@ani_news) May 22, 2015the misuse of investigative agencies, is now an event of the past: I&B Minister Arun Jaitley — ANI (@ani_news) May 22, 2015 sarkaar ne shanivaar ko spasht kiya ki 1 july se iskar ritern daakhil karne or sthaayee khaataa sankhya (pan) hasil karne ke liye aadhaar or pan ko aapas main jodna anivaary hoga

 sheersh adaalat ne iskar adhinium main kiye gaye us praavdhaan ko vaid mana he jisamen pan card aavanton or iskar ritern daakhil karne ke liye aadhaar ko anivaary kiya gaya he, lekin niztaa ke adhikaar se jude maamle par sanvaidhanik peeth kaa faisla aane tak iske kriyanvayan par aanshik sthagan laga diya
 The Central Board of Direct Taxes (CBDT), the policy making body of the Income Tax Department, issued a statement on Saturday clarifying that the Supreme Court in its judgment on Friday only gave partial relief to those who do not have an Aadhaar number or who have Aadhaar The tax authorities will not cancel the PAN of those people who have not registered
 sibiditi ne supreme court ke faisle ke bare main teen binduon kaa spashtikaran jari kiya he
 This explanation was given to the taxpayers to remove any apprehension from the Supreme Court's decision
 1 july, 2017 se prayek vyakti jo aadhaar paane kaa paatr he uske liye iskar ritern daakhil karne yaa phir pan ke liye aavedan karne main apane aadhaar number kaa ullekh athwa aadhaar panjikaran sambandhi idi number kaa ullekh karnaa anivaary hoga
 The CBDT has said, 'on July 1, 2017, any person who has been allotted a PAN number and whoever has an Aadhaar number or is eligible to get an Aadhaar number is required to add their Aadhaar number with PAN The number has to be reported to the Income Tax Administration
 ' The department has also given clarification about what will happen if a person does not have an Aadhaar number or if the Aadhaar number is not mentioned
 vibhaag ne kaha he, 'is maamle main sheersh adaalat ne keval aanshik raahat di he
 This relief has been given to those who do not have Aadhaar or who are not willing to take Aadhaar at present
 aise logon ke maamle main pan number nirast nahin kiya jayega, taaki iskar adhinium ke tahat pan number kaa ullekh nahin karne sambandhi duusare niyamon kaa khamiyaja unhen nahin bhugatna pade
 ' ek varisht iskar adhikari ne bataaya yadi pan ko nirast kar diya jaataa he, to sambandhit vyakti apane saamaanya banking or vittiya parichaalan nahin kar paaegaa, isliye yah raahat di gai he
 But it has been clarified that it will be mandatory to file Aadhaar return from July 1 and mention Aadhaar if a new PAN is to be created
 varisht adhikari ne kaha ki sheersh adaalat ke shuukravaar ke faisle kaa kanoon mantralay, vitt mantralay, sibiditi or iskar vibhaag ke adhikariyon ne adhyayan kiya he or uske baad hi yah spashtikaran jari kiya gaya he
 The comments sarkaar ne vitt adhinium 2017 ke tahat karadaataaon ke liye aadhaar number athwa aadhaar panjikaran aavedan sankhya ko iskar ritern daakhil karte samay ullekh karnaa anivaary kar diya
 Along with this, Aadhaar has been made mandatory in the application for PAN from 1 July 2017

 ) iskar vibhaag kii niti nirmaataa sanstha kendriya pratyaksh kar board (sibiditi) ne shanivaar ko ek vaktavy jari kar spasht kiya ki supreme court ne shuukravaar ko apane faisle main keval un logon ko aanshik raahat di he, jinke paas aadhaar number nahin he athwa jinhone aadhaar main panjikaran nahin karaayaa he, aise main kar adhikari un logon ke pan ko nirast nahin karenge
 The CBDT has issued a three-point clarification regarding the Supreme Court's decision
 karadaataaon main supreme court ke faisle se kisi tarah kii ashanka ko dur karne ke liye yah spashtikaran diya gaya
 From July 1, 2017, every person who is eligible to get Aadhaar will be required to mention their Aadhaar number or mention their Aadhaar registration ID number in filing income tax return or applying for PAN

 ' vibhaag ne is bare main bhi spashtikaran diya he ki yadi kisi vyakti ke paas aadhaar number nahin he athwa aadhaar number kaa ullekh nahin kiya jaataa he, to uskaa kya hoga
 The department has said, 'the apex court has given only partial relief in this case
 yah raahat un logon ko di gai he, jinke paas aadhaar nahin he yaa jo philhal aadhaar nahin lenaa chaah rahe hai
 In the case of such people, the PAN number will not be canceled, so that they do not have to bear the brunt of other rules not mentioning the PAN number under the Income Tax Act
 ' a senior income tax official told that if the PAN is canceled, the person concerned will not be able to carry out his normal banking and financial operations, hence this relief has been granted

 Sri Lankan legend Muttiah Muralitharan, one of the greatest but most controversial spinners of his generation, retired his 18-year-old Test cricket amid an influx of emotions with an unprecedented figure of 800 wickets on Thursday
 srilanka ne bharat par 10 wicket kii jeet ke saath apane is hero bejod vidaai thi jabaki is 38 varshiya of spinner ne match main aath wicket ke saath 800 test wicket ke aankade ke saath nijee taur par match ko yaadgaar bana diya
 It was a very emotional occasion for this great spinner who was given a guard of honor by the players of both teams during the match
 murali ke bejod karier kaa jashn manaane ke liye prayek din match kii shuruuaat se pehle pataakhe chode gayi or unke parijan bhi is lamhe ke gavaah bane
 He took 800 wickets in 133 Tests and 515 wickets in 337 odis, which is the record for most wickets in both formats of the game
 murali haalanki ab test maichon main nahin khelenge lekin unhone bharat, srilanka or bangladesh kii mejabani main hone vaale 2011 ekadivasiy vishwa cap main khilne kaa vikalp khulaa rakhaa he
 Muralitharan's career, however, has not been untouched by controversies and during his unmatched career, umpires also accused him of throwing the ball
 vah bhale hi duniya ke sabase safal gendbaaj rahe hon lekin vivaad unke karier kaa abhinn hissaa rahe
 Muralitharan, who made his 1992 debut against Australia, became the reason for the early discussion due to his strange bowling action
 karier kii shuruuaat se hi unka ection hameshaa andeh ke ghere main rahaa or padaarpan ke teen saal baad 1995-96 main australia daure par ampire derel hair ne thro karne ke liye unki gend ko nobal qaraar diya
 The International Cricket Council then recommended a biomechanical analysis at West Australia University and found that their action caused the illusion of throwing
 yah maamla haalanki yaheen samaapt nahin hua or 1998-99 ke austrailia daure par ek baar phir unke ection par andeh jataayaa gaya or is baar rose emrsan ne unke ection par sawaal uthaaye
 Murali was then sent to Perth and England for trial where his action was justified
 murali par haalanki iskaa koi asar nahin padaa or vah westeindies ke kartney walsh ke 519 wicket ke aankado ko paar karke test maichon main sarvaadhik wicket chatakaane vaale gendbaaj bane
 Murali's wicket was fought with Australia's legendary leg-spinner Shane Warne and he held the record for most wickets between the two
 warn ne 708 wicket ke saath test cricket ko alavida kaha jis aankade ko murali ne disambar 2007 main england ke khilaaf candi main apane gharelu maidan main peeche chhod diya
 Murali then became the highest wicket-taker in ODI cricket in 2009, surpassing Pakistan's fast bowler Wasim Akram's 502-ball record
 yah champion spinner 2007 vishwa cap main kaaphi kuch nahin kar paaya or ab yah dekhnaa hoga ki vah 2011 vishwa cap main khelkar apni team ko doosraa vishwa cap dilaane main madad karte hai yaa nahin
 He said it is difficult for him to throw long spells and he is likely to play in Twenty20 cricket
 vah indian premier lig main champion chennai superkings kii ore se khelte hai jise dakshin africa main sitambar main twanti-20 champions lig main hissaa lenaa he

 ye nattejey hai india today or nilsan ke taaja survey ke
 According to the survey, in the opinion of 21 percent people, Narendra Modi will prove to be the best Prime Minister of the country
 india today or nilsan ke survey main janata se ek or sawaal poocha gaya- agar bijepi gujarat vidhansabha chunaav jitati he to kya bijepi pradhanmantri kii ummidavaari ke liye narendra modi kaa naam aage badhayegi? iske jawaab main 55 fisadi janata ne kaha haa jabaki 25 fisadi janata ne kaha naa
 Narendra Modi's magic on people, how the magic of Narendra Modi has gone on people, you can see this in the survey figures
 pradhanmantri pad ke liye modi pehali pasand hai or baaki log to unase bahut peeche hai
 Narendra Modi is the first choice of 21 percent people for the post of Prime Minister
 duusare number par he atal bihari bajpeyi kaa naam
 17 percent people have described Atal Bihari Bajpayee as their first choice
 10 fisadi log chaahate hai ki rahul gandhi agle pradhanmantri bane jabaki 8 fisadi log chaahate hai ki laalkrishna adwani bane desh ke agle pradhanmantri
 Only 6 per cent of the opinion of the nation's Prime Minister Manmohan Singh was in favor
 vahiin upie kii cheirperson sonia gandhi ko 6 fisadi janata ne bataaya pradhanmantri pad ke liye pehali pasand
 4 percent of the people said that Mayawati was their first choice for PM, 4 percent said that Mulayam Singh Yadav should be the next Prime Minister
 desh ke sabase achche mukhyamantri hai modisrve ke nattejey bataate hai ki res main baaki logon se bahut aage chal rahe hai narendra modi
 Recently the RSS had described Nitish Kumar as a better Chief Minister than Narendra Modi, Nitish Kumar may have been very happy at that time
 lekin india today or nilsan survey ke nattejey nitish kumaar ko niraash hi karenge
 According to the survey, Narendra Modi is the best Chief Minister of the country
 duusare number par he nitish kumaar kaa naam
 Akhilesh Yadav is at number three and Delhi Chief Minister Sheila Dixit is at number four
 india today or nilsan ne 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaavon ko dekhte hue desh kii janata kaa mood bhaanpane ke liye hi ye survey kiye the
 The survey was conducted on 125 Lok Sabha seats of 19 states between 6 July and 20 July
 survey main 15 hajaar 827 votaron kii raay lee gai
 The survey covered two assembly constituencies of each Lok Sabha seat and voters went door-to-door during the survey
 modi ke raste main kaante bhi kam nahinsrvey ke aankade to modi ko khush kar sakate hai lekin siyasat ke raste par unke liye phool kam or kaante zyaada hai
 Modi, who has moved away from Gujarat and attacked the central government, has made it clear in a way that his eyes are on the throne of Delhi
 india today or nilsan ke survey kii maane to pradhanmantri pad ke liye desh kii zyaadaatar janata kii pasand bhi modi hi hai
 But Modi's path is not easy
 khud bijepi main hi unke kai virdohi hai, jo kisi bhi keemat par nahin chahenge ki modi kaa naam piem in vatting ke taur par rakhaa jaae
 There is no dearth of Modi's opponents in Gujarat itself, in the past, posters were pasted in Gujarat against Modi, in which he was described as a victim of law
 modi kaa virodh karne vaale keshubhai patel ne to alag party bana lee, vahiin unke raajnneetik virdohi sanjay joshi ko party ne baahar kaa rasta dikhaa diya
 The clear message was that only Narendra Modi's walks in BJP
 sahyogiyon ko manaanaa nahin hoga aasananarendra modi kaa naam bijepi manjuur bhi kar le to endie ko unke naam par raji karnaa behad mushkil he
 Nitish Kumar did not allow him to enter Bihar in the last assembly elections, then in the past, he had clearly stated that the PM candidate in the NDA should be secular
 nitish ne modi par nishaanaa saadhaa to jediu ne baqayada modi ke khilaaf morcha khol diya, endie se naata todane tak kii dhamkee de daali
 When JDU waged a war of words, the Modi camp of BJP also took a beating
 endie main modi ke naam par sir phutuval kii naubat ai to is gathbandhan ke virdohi bhi aag main ghi daalane lage
 In the name of Narendra Modi, there is often a fierce battle in the NDA, so what to talk about other parties
 congress to modi ke naam par hi bidak jaati he
 The idea of avoiding Modi is that in the past, Shahid Siddiqui, the leader of Samajwadi Party and editor of New World Urdu, published an interview of Narendra Modi in his newspaper
 jisamen modi ne kaha tha- agar main gujarat dange kaa gunahagaar hum to mujhe faansee par lataka do

 duusari taraf abhi pragna se kahata he ki kuch der ke liye vah bhul janaa chahta he ki vah purab kii garlfriend he, pragna bhi man hi man yahi sochati he
 After this, both of them do a romantic dance, seeing that Dadi, Maid and Purab are happy while Alia and Tanu get upset
 iske baad tanu nikhil ko phone karke apni madad ke liye bulaati he
 On the other hand Tanu complains to Alia that her plan fails, Pragya has cast a spell on Abhi
 ab vah uski taraf dekhegaa bhi nahin
 Aaliya tells him that Tanu himself is responsible for all this
 use pragna ke ghar jaakar use bura-bhala nahin kahana tha
 Due to her provocation, Pragya reached there wearing a western dress and has Abhi on her side
 vah tanu se kahati he ki vah haar gai he or ab use apni haar kaa matam manaanaa chahie
 The comments pragna ke mekaover se abhi ke impress hone se purab khush hota he ki tanu or aalia ko jabardast jhatka mila he
 He sees Dadi and Maid at the party and says that seeing Abhi's face, she feels that Pragya is not her former girlfriend
 vah daadi se kahata he ki vah jald hi pragna se apane afaire naatak khatm kar degaa
 Abhi on the other hand tells Pragya that for some time he wants to forget that she is the girlfriend of the East, Pragya also thinks the same
 iske baad donon ek romantic dance karte hai, jise dekh daadi, daasi or purab khush hote hai vahiin aalia or tanu pareshaan ho jate hai
 Tanu then calls Nikhil for his help
 pragna ke mekaover se abhi ke impress hone se purab khush hota he ki tanu or aalia ko jabardast jhatka mila he

 Are we really talking about justice or do Congress vs BJP in the name of justice? dangon or narsanhaaron ke insaaf kii baat jab bhi aati he vah vahaan bhi pahunchati he jahaan isaki baat nahin hoti he
 His voice is resonating in Pune and Alwar as well as in Bulandshahr
 sajjan kumaar ne congress kii praathmik sadsyta se istipha de diya he
 Sajjan Kumar is neither one nor Sajjan Kumar is in a team
 17 disambar ko jab 84 ke aanshik insaaf kii baat ho rahi thi, usee din 84 banaam 2002 kaa hisaab ho rahaa tha usee din maharashtra ke sholapur main ek pita chupchaap duniya chhod gaya
 Mohsin Sheikh, son of Sadiq Sheikh was killed by the mob
 63 saal ke sadiq shaikh ne 2014 se apane bete mohsin shaikh kii hatya ke insaaf ke liye apni taraf se bahut ladaai ladi
 Mohsin from Solapur was a lone earner and worked at Wipro in Pune
 soshal media par shivaji or bal thakare ko lekar aapattijanak tippanee ke virodh main ek bheed sadak par utar gai thi
 This crowd belonged to the Hindu Rashtra Sena which had gathered for its resistance meeting
 vahaan se guzarate hue mohsin shaikh ko lohe kii rod or haaki stick se petakar maar diya gaya
 She was accompanied by another youngster Riyaz Sheikh, who had come to Gambhir Chote
 donon hi iti ejeeniyar the or khaanaa khaakar apane kamare par laut rahe the
 From then until 17 December, Sadiq Sheikh had broken down fighting for the justice of his son's murder
 is ladaai main paise kii itani tangi ho gai ki you-tub par baqayada sarkaar se apil kii thi ki paise die jaaen or bete mobin ko naukari di jaae
 In June 2014, the Congress was in government, then got 5 lakh compensation, later the government changed, nothing was found
 sadiq shaikh ne bijepi sarkaar ko kai patr likhe, magar madad nahin mili
 Interviewed the media so that the matter reached the government, the matter did not reach
 sadik shaikh ne 6 march 2018 main bambai hai court main cese file kiya tha
 On 12 April 2018, a notice was issued to the Government of Maharashtra that they should be compensated
 sadik shaikh ne 30 lakh 90 hazaar muaavze kii maang kii thi
 In June 2018, the Maharashtra government passed a resolution that 5 lakh state government and 5 lakh central government would pay compensation
 lekin june ke prastaav ke baad bhi november 2018 tak ek nayaa paisa nahin mila
 So Sadiq Sheikh went to court again
 28 november ko court ne kaha ki inhen ek hafte ke bheetar muawza diya jaae
 During that time, the court asked the government why compensation had not been received yet
 iske jawaab main sarkaar ne kaha ki sadik shaikh kii pahchaan sthapit nahin ho paa rahi thi jabaki sadik shaikh kii taraf se soochna adhikaar ke tahat sawaal kiya gaya tha or jawaab mila tha
 That is, there was identity while answering RTI but identity could not be established giving the amount of compensation
 yah kahani lambii he magar dhiraj se sunenge to insaaf kii dramebaazi samaj aa jaaegi
 Received money a week ago
 chah maheene lag gaye
 In the meantime, the cash-strapped illness beset Sadiq Sheikh
 majabuuran ve aryuvedic chikitsa karaane lage kyonki yah sasta tha
 This is the condition of justice
 sadik shaikh ne sholapur main dam tod diya
 The Pune police has charged the Chief of Hindu Rashtra Dhananjay Desai and 23 others for the murder of Mohsin
 dhananjay desai jail main he
 In 2017, the Bombay High Court granted surety to the three accused in the case, when the order was severely criticized for its language and context
 justise mridula bhatkar ne jamaanat main likhaa ki Transcript from Dhananjay Desai's provocative speech shows that he instigated a sense of religious discrimination
 aavedak yaa aropiyon kii mohsin ke khilaaf nijee shatruta jaisi koi or manshaa nahin thi
 It was the mistake of the deceased that he belonged to other religion
 main is baat ko aaropee ke haq main maanati hum
 Not only this, the accused or the applicant does not have a criminal past
 aisa prathit hota he ki dharm ke naam unhen uksaaya gaya or unhone hatya kar di
 Sadiq Sheikh challenged the bail order in the Supreme Court
 farvari 2018 main supreme court ne zamaanat radd kar di
 a website called Live Law has referred to the Supreme Court's comment in its report, with Justice SA Bovde and Justice l Nageshwara sending the trio to jail, saying that the communities involved in the attacks can be understood as a reference or reference but It is beyond comprehension why it was written in the judgment that the death of the deceased i
e
 Mohsin was so much that he belonged to other religion
 main is baat ko aaropee ke paksh main maanata hum, hamen is baat par shaq he ki adaalat puri tarah se is baat ko lekar sajag he ki bharat ek bahudharm desh he
 One cannot comment in such a way as to indicate that the verdict was specific to a community
 supreme court kaa faisla to kaaphi samay baad aayaa tha lekin hamane is par tabhi charchaa kii thi jab bambai hai court kii zamaanat kaa aadesh diya tha
 Faizan Mustafa was with us and reviewed it
 17 janvari 2017 ke prime time main faizan mustafa ne bambai hai court kii jaj ke aadesh par apni raay di thi
 Justice also has its own politics
 bahes karne vaale hindu kii taraf se bahes karte hai, muslim kii taraf se bahes karte hai
 But whoever suffers, no religion is used
 na islam na hindu
 He lives by fighting the trust of a few while fighting alone
 sisakata he
 So those celebrating for justice should once ask Jagdish Kaur whether she struggled for 34 years or the spokespersons appearing in TV
 balki wo na milen to unhen mohsin kii maa shabana sadiq sheikh se poochna chahie, wo bhi na mil paaen to bulandshahr main maar die gaye inspector subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani ji se poochna chahie
 The battle of Shabana and Rajni is also a lonely battle like Zakia Jaffrey and Jagdish Kaur
 aapako bheed kii vah tasviir to yaad hi hogi, gaay ke naam par jamaa bheed ne inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya kar di
 It has been 16–17 days since the main accused has not been arrested
 is bich mukhya aaropee ne whatsap ke zarie ek bayaan bhi jari kiya jo tivi par chalaa
 In this case, senior police officers were transferred but the main accused was not arrested
 mukhyamantri ne ghatana ke baad ek baithak bhi bulaai thi jiske bare main press release jari hui to subodh kumaar singh ke bare main koi zikr nahin tha, is baat kaa tha ki gau hatya karne waalon par sakht karrwai kii jaae
 Later Chief Minister Adityanath called the victim's family to Lucknow, Subodh Kumar Singh's wife Rajni, his sons went to meet him but the main accused has not yet been caught
 aaj hi subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ko lekar 80 se adhik sevanivrutt adhikariyon ne khulaa patr likhaa he
 These include officers of IFS, IAS and IPS, Forest Service and Revenue Service
 kuch kai mahatvapurn mulkon main rajdoot rah chuke hai
 Former National Security Advisor Shiv Shankar Menon is also on this list
 is patr main mukhyamantri aditya nath kii aalochana kii gai he, un par dharmandhta kaa paksh lene kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he or istife kii maang kii gai he
 These officers have written that they are not from any political party
 samvidhan ke mulyon ke alaava kisi or vichaardhaara main yakeen nahin rakhte
 i want to read some part of this letter for you - On December 3, 2018, mob violence was carried out in Bulandshahr, Uttar Pradesh with malice
 isamen bheed ko shant karne kii koshish kar rahe upi police ke ek bahadur afasar kii nrushans hatya kar di gai
 This became the most terrible turn in the direction of hate politics
 ye dikhaata he ki desh ke sabase aabaadi vaale rajya uttarapradesh main shashan ke moulik siddhanton, sanvaidhanik naitikta or maanviya saamaajik vyavhaar ko taak par rakh diya gaya he
 The chief minister of the state is promoting the domination of fundamentalism and majoritarianism
 ye ek aisa agenda he jo duusari har chiz par haaavee he
 According to the letter such incidents have happened in Uttar Pradesh before but till now we believed that whenever a political party forms a government, it rules with responsibility keeping aside the partisan political agenda to increase its political acceptability
 lekin bulandshahr kii ghatana se pehle upi main muslim samudaay ko daraane or alag-thalag karne kii lagaataar koshishen hoti rahi hai
 With Yogi Adityanath as the Chief Minister, our faith has been proved wrong and hooliganism and cheating have joined the mainstream of governance to not only intimidate the minorities but to teach a lesson to every person, police and administration who along with the minority community Dare to behave equally
 jab tak inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ke maamle main jaanch puri nahin ho jaati tab tak kisi nattejey par pahunchnaa jaldbaazi hogi lekin isamen koi shaq nahin he ki jis tarah unki hatya hui usamen kuch bhi swaabhaavik yaa swat: sfoort nahin tha
 There is also no doubt about which political elements encouraged and instigated the violence
 jaanboojhkar bahusnkhyakon kii taaqat ko dikhaane kii koshish hui taaki ilaake main rahane vaale muslim samudaayon ko sandesh diya ja sake ki unhen dar main rahanaa hoga, wo bahusankhyak samudaay ke saanskrithik farmaanon ko maane or khud ko unase kamatar maane
 It is also written in the letter that the police and civil administration have succumbed to the distorted political system
 wo samvidhan ke prati apni praathmik vafadaari or kaanoon ke raaj ko bhul chuke hai jabaki unka sanvaidhanik darja unhen abhootpurv taaqat detaa he
 If they had taken steps to curb the growing fear of the Hindutva brigade, the violence could have been definitely prevented
 lekin unhone naa sirf gundgardee karne waalon ke hausale ko badhane diya or unhen raajnneetik taaqat hasil karne diya balki apni lachar karrwai se unke man se kaanoon ke dar ko hataane main bhi madad kii
 Even now, if the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary, DM and district police officers stand together, this deadly political agenda can be exposed, its masterminds can be identified and the perpetrators of violence should be put in the dock Can
 in adhikariyon ke saamne samvidhan kii shapath ko puraa karne kaa mauka he or ucch naagarik sevaaon se nagarikon ko jo ummiden hai unhen puraa karne kaa avasar he
 The comments khat main pradhanmantri kaa aahvaan karte hue likhaa gaya he ki hamaare pradhanmantri jo apane chunavi abhiyaanon main ye kehete nahin thakte ki bharat kaa samvidhan hi ekmaatr kitaab he jisaki wo puja karte hai, wo bhi is maamle main chuppi saadhe hue hai jabaki unke chune hue mukhyamantri usee samvidhan ke saath khilwaad kar rahe hai
 It is clear that constitutional morality has no value for the Sangh Parivar and it considers the idea of majority domination
 ye ek bahut hi gambhir samay he or ham ise yon hi nahin chhod sakate
 We demand all citizens to unite against this politics of hate and division
 ham maang karte hai ki uttarapradesh ke mukhyamantri samvidhan ke paalan main naakaam rahane ke liye istifa den jis samvidhan ko lagu karne kii unhone shapath khai he
 We know that this will happen only when we together raise public sentiments and force them to resign, making them feel responsible for their work
 ham mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv or ucch naagarik sevaaon ke sabhi sadasyon ko yaad dilaanaa chaahate hai ki ye unka sanvaidhanik daayitv he ki wo apane raajnneetik aakaaon ke vikrut adeshon ke bajaay bina dare kaanoon kaa raaj sthapit karen

 majabuuran ve aryuvedic chikitsa karaane lage kyonki yah sasta tha
 This is the condition of justice
 sadik shaikh ne sholapur main dam tod diya
 The Pune police has charged the Chief of Hindu Rashtra Dhananjay Desai and 23 others for the murder of Mohsin
 dhananjay desai jail main he
 In 2017, the Bombay High Court granted surety to the three accused in the case, when the order was severely criticized for its language and context
 justise mridula bhatkar ne jamaanat main likhaa ki Transcript from Dhananjay Desai's provocative speech shows that he instigated a sense of religious discrimination
 aavedak yaa aropiyon kii mohsin ke khilaaf nijee shatruta jaisi koi or manshaa nahin thi
 It was the mistake of the deceased that he belonged to other religion
 main is baat ko aaropee ke haq main maanati hum
 Not only this, the accused or the applicant does not have a criminal past
 aisa prathit hota he ki dharm ke naam unhen uksaaya gaya or unhone hatya kar di
 Sadiq Sheikh challenged the bail order in the Supreme Court
 farvari 2018 main supreme court ne zamaanat radd kar di
 a website called Live Law has referred to the Supreme Court's comment in its report, with Justice SA Bovde and Justice l Nageshwara sending the trio to jail, saying that the communities involved in the attacks can be understood as a reference or reference but It is beyond comprehension why it was written in the judgment that the death of the deceased i
e
 Mohsin was so much that he belonged to other religion
 main is baat ko aaropee ke paksh main maanata hum, hamen is baat par shaq he ki adaalat puri tarah se is baat ko lekar sajag he ki bharat ek bahudharm desh he
 One cannot comment in such a way as to indicate that the verdict was specific to a community
 supreme court kaa faisla to kaaphi samay baad aayaa tha lekin hamane is par tabhi charchaa kii thi jab bambai hai court kii zamaanat kaa aadesh diya tha
 Faizan Mustafa was with us and reviewed it
 17 janvari 2017 ke prime time main faizan mustafa ne bambai hai court kii jaj ke aadesh par apni raay di thi
 Justice also has its own politics
 bahes karne vaale hindu kii taraf se bahes karte hai, muslim kii taraf se bahes karte hai
 But whoever suffers, no religion is used
 na islam na hindu
 He lives by fighting the trust of a few while fighting alone
 sisakata he
 So those celebrating for justice should once ask Jagdish Kaur whether she struggled for 34 years or the spokespersons appearing in TV
 balki wo na milen to unhen mohsin kii maa shabana sadiq sheikh se poochna chahie, wo bhi na mil paaen to bulandshahr main maar die gaye inspector subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani ji se poochna chahie
 The battle of Shabana and Rajni is also a lonely battle like Zakia Jaffrey and Jagdish Kaur
 aapako bheed kii vah tasviir to yaad hi hogi, gaay ke naam par jamaa bheed ne inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya kar di
 It has been 16–17 days since the main accused has not been arrested
 is bich mukhya aaropee ne whatsap ke zarie ek bayaan bhi jari kiya jo tivi par chalaa
 In this case, senior police officers were transferred but the main accused was not arrested
 mukhyamantri ne ghatana ke baad ek baithak bhi bulaai thi jiske bare main press release jari hui to subodh kumaar singh ke bare main koi zikr nahin tha, is baat kaa tha ki gau hatya karne waalon par sakht karrwai kii jaae
 Later Chief Minister Adityanath called the victim's family to Lucknow, Subodh Kumar Singh's wife Rajni, his sons went to meet him but the main accused has not yet been caught
 aaj hi subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ko lekar 80 se adhik sevanivrutt adhikariyon ne khulaa patr likhaa he
 These include officers of IFS, IAS and IPS, Forest Service and Revenue Service
 kuch kai mahatvapurn mulkon main rajdoot rah chuke hai
 Former National Security Advisor Shiv Shankar Menon is also on this list
 is patr main mukhyamantri aditya nath kii aalochana kii gai he, un par dharmandhta kaa paksh lene kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he or istife kii maang kii gai he
 These officers have written that they are not from any political party
 samvidhan ke mulyon ke alaava kisi or vichaardhaara main yakeen nahin rakhte
 i want to read some part of this letter for you - On December 3, 2018, mob violence was carried out in Bulandshahr, Uttar Pradesh with malice
 isamen bheed ko shant karne kii koshish kar rahe upi police ke ek bahadur afasar kii nrushans hatya kar di gai
 This became the most terrible turn in the direction of hate politics
 ye dikhaata he ki desh ke sabase aabaadi vaale rajya uttarapradesh main shashan ke moulik siddhanton, sanvaidhanik naitikta or maanviya saamaajik vyavhaar ko taak par rakh diya gaya he
 The chief minister of the state is promoting the domination of fundamentalism and majoritarianism
 ye ek aisa agenda he jo duusari har chiz par haaavee he
 According to the letter such incidents have happened in Uttar Pradesh before but till now we believed that whenever a political party forms a government, it rules with responsibility keeping aside the partisan political agenda to increase its political acceptability
 lekin bulandshahr kii ghatana se pehle upi main muslim samudaay ko daraane or alag-thalag karne kii lagaataar koshishen hoti rahi hai
 With Yogi Adityanath as the Chief Minister, our faith has been proved wrong and hooliganism and cheating have joined the mainstream of governance to not only intimidate the minorities but to teach a lesson to every person, police and administration who along with the minority community Dare to behave equally
 jab tak inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ke maamle main jaanch puri nahin ho jaati tab tak kisi nattejey par pahunchnaa jaldbaazi hogi lekin isamen koi shaq nahin he ki jis tarah unki hatya hui usamen kuch bhi swaabhaavik yaa swat: sfoort nahin tha
 There is also no doubt about which political elements encouraged and instigated the violence
 jaanboojhkar bahusnkhyakon kii taaqat ko dikhaane kii koshish hui taaki ilaake main rahane vaale muslim samudaayon ko sandesh diya ja sake ki unhen dar main rahanaa hoga, wo bahusankhyak samudaay ke saanskrithik farmaanon ko maane or khud ko unase kamatar maane
 It is also written in the letter that the police and civil administration have succumbed to the distorted political system
 wo samvidhan ke prati apni praathmik vafadaari or kaanoon ke raaj ko bhul chuke hai jabaki unka sanvaidhanik darja unhen abhootpurv taaqat detaa he
 If they had taken steps to curb the growing fear of the Hindutva brigade, the violence could have been definitely prevented
 lekin unhone naa sirf gundgardee karne waalon ke hausale ko badhane diya or unhen raajnneetik taaqat hasil karne diya balki apni lachar karrwai se unke man se kaanoon ke dar ko hataane main bhi madad kii
 Even now, if the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary, DM and district police officers stand together, this deadly political agenda can be exposed, its masterminds can be identified and the perpetrators of violence should be put in the dock Can
 in adhikariyon ke saamne samvidhan kii shapath ko puraa karne kaa mauka he or ucch naagarik sevaaon se nagarikon ko jo ummiden hai unhen puraa karne kaa avasar he
 The comments khat main pradhanmantri kaa aahvaan karte hue likhaa gaya he ki hamaare pradhanmantri jo apane chunavi abhiyaanon main ye kehete nahin thakte ki bharat kaa samvidhan hi ekmaatr kitaab he jisaki wo puja karte hai, wo bhi is maamle main chuppi saadhe hue hai jabaki unke chune hue mukhyamantri usee samvidhan ke saath khilwaad kar rahe hai
 It is clear that constitutional morality has no value for the Sangh Parivar and it considers the idea of majority domination
 ye ek bahut hi gambhir samay he or ham ise yon hi nahin chhod sakate
 We demand all citizens to unite against this politics of hate and division
 ham maang karte hai ki uttarapradesh ke mukhyamantri samvidhan ke paalan main naakaam rahane ke liye istifa den jis samvidhan ko lagu karne kii unhone shapath khai he
 We know that this will happen only when we together raise public sentiments and force them to resign, making them feel responsible for their work
 ham mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv or ucch naagarik sevaaon ke sabhi sadasyon ko yaad dilaanaa chaahate hai ki ye unka sanvaidhanik daayitv he ki wo apane raajnneetik aakaaon ke vikrut adeshon ke bajaay bina dare kaanoon kaa raaj sthapit karen
 Simultaneously, the Allahabad High Court has been requested to take suo motu cognizance of this incident and order a judicial inquiry under its supervision
 pune police ne mohsin kii hatya ke aarope main hindu raashtra ke chif dhananjay desai or 23 anya ko chargeshit kiya he
 Dhananjay Desai is in jail
 2017 main bambai hoicourt ne is maamle main teen aropiyon ko zamaanat de di thi, tab aadesh kii bhashaa or sandarbh ko lekar kaaphi aalochana hui thi
 Justice Mridula Bhatkar wrote in bail that dhananjay desai ke bhadakaau bhaashan se transcript se pataa chalata he ki usne dharmik bhedbhaav kii bhaavana ko bhadakaayaa
 The applicant or the accused had no other motive such as personal enmity against Mohsin
 mritak kii yahi galati thi ki vah anya dharm kaa he
 i believe this to be in favor of the accused
 yahi nahin aaropee yaa aavedak kaa aapraadhik ateet nahin he
 He appears to have been instigated in the name of religion and murdered
 jamaanat ke aadesh ko sadik shaikh ne supreme court main chunauti di
 In February 2018, the Supreme Court canceled the bail
 live lau naam kii website ne apni report main supreme court kii tippanee kaa zikr kiya he, justise ese bovade or justise el nageshwara ne in teenon ko jail bhejte hue kaha tha ki hamale main shaamil pakshon ke samudaayon kaa sandarbh yaa zikr samajha ja saktaa he lekin yah baat samaj se pare he ki kyon faisle main likhaa gaya ki marane vaale kaa yani mohsin kaa kasoor itnaa hi tha ki vah anya dharm kaa tha
 i believe this in favor of the accused, we doubt that the court is fully aware that India is a multi-religious country
 is tarah kii tippanee nahin kar sakati he ki jisase lage ki faisla ek samudaay ke prati khaas najariya rakhata tha
 The Supreme Court's decision came after a long time, but we discussed it only when the Bombay High Court was ordered to bail
 faizan mustafa hamaare saath the or unhone is baat kii samiksha kii thi
 In the prime time of 17 January 2017, Faizan Mustafa gave his opinion on the order of the Bombay High Court judge
 insaaf kii bhi apni raajnneeti he
 Debaters argue on behalf of Hindus, argue on behalf of Muslims
 lekin jo peedit hota he uske kaam koi dharm nahin aata he
 Neither Islam nor Hindu
 wo akelaa ladata hua chand logon ke bharose ke sahare jeeta he
 Sob isliye insaaf ke liye jashn manaane waalon ko ek baar jagadish cor se poochna chahie ki 34 saal sangharsh unhone kiya yaa tivi main aane vaale pravaktaaon ne kiya
 Rather, if they do not meet, they should ask Mohsin's mother Shabana Sadiq Sheikh, if they cannot find it, then they should ask Rajni ji, wife of Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh, who was killed in Bulandshahr
 shabana or rajani kii ladaai bhi zakiya jaafaree or jagadish cor kii tarah akele kii ladaai he
 You must remember that picture of the crowd, the mob gathered in the name of the cow killed Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh
 16-17 din ho gaye mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 Meanwhile, the main accused also released a statement through whatsapp which went on TV
 is cese main police ke varisht adhikariyon kaa tabadalaa ho gaya lekin mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 The Chief Minister had also called a meeting after the incident about which there was no mention of Subodh Kumar Singh when the press release was issued, that strict action should be taken against those who killed cow
 baad main mukhyamantri adityanath ne peedit parivaar ko lakhanu bulaayaa, subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani, unke bete unase milane gaye lekin abhi tak mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya he
 Today, more than 80 retired officials have written an open letter regarding the murder of Subodh Kumar Singh
 inamen iesces, iees or ipies, van seva or rajasav seva ke adhikari hai
 Some have been ambassadors in many important countries
 is suchi main purv rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar shiv shankar menon bhi hai
 The letter criticizes Chief Minister Aditya Nath, accusing him of favoring bigotry and demanding his resignation
 in afasaron ne likhaa he ki ve kisi raajnneetik dal se nahin hai
 Do not believe in any ideology other than the values of the constitution
 is patr kaa kuch hissaa aapke liye padhanaa chahta hum- 3 disambar, 2018 ko uttarapradesh ke bulandshahr main durbhaavna ke saath bheed kii hinsa ko anjaam diya gaya
 In this, a brave officer of the UP police, who was trying to calm the crowd, was brutally murdered
 ye nafrat kii raajnneeti kii disha main sabase bhayanak mode ban gaya
 It shows that Uttar Pradesh, the most populous state in the country, has kept the fundamental principles of governance, constitutional ethics and human social behavior at bay
 rajya ke mukhyamantri kattarta or bahusankhyakwaad ke varchasv ko badhaava de rahe hai
 This is an agenda that dominates everything else
 khat ke mutabik aisi ghatnaayen uttarapradesh main pehle bhi hui hai lekin abhi tak hamen vishwaas tha ki jab bhi koi raajnneetik dal sarkaar banaata he to wo pakshpaat bhare raajnneetik agenda ko alag rakhkar zimmedaari ke saath shashan karata he taaki uski raajnneetik sweekaaryata bade
 But before the Bulandshahr incident, there have been constant attempts to intimidate and isolate the Muslim community in UP
 yogi adityanath ke mukhyamantri rahete hamaara wo vishwaas galat sabit hua he or gundgardee or thagi shashan kii mukhyadhara main shaamil ho gaye hai taaki na sirf alpsankhyakon ko daraaya ja sake balki har us vyakti, police or prashasan ko sabak sikhaaya ja sake jo alpsankhyak samudaay ke saath barabari kaa vyavhaar karne kii himmat kare
 Until the investigation into the murder of Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh is complete, it is too early to come to any conclusion, but there is no doubt that nothing was natural or spontaneous in the manner in which he was killed
 is baat main bhi koi shaq nahin he ki kin raajnneetik tatwon ne hinsa ko badhaava or uksaava diya
 There was a deliberate attempt to show the strength of the majority in order to give a message to the Muslim communities living in the area that they have to live in fear, accept the cultural decrees of the majority community and consider themselves inferior to them
 khat main ye bhi likhaa gaya he ki police or naagarik prashasan vikrut raajnneetik tantra ke aage jhuk chukaa he
 They have forgotten their primary loyalty to the Constitution and the rule of law, while their constitutional status gives them unprecedented power
 agar wo hindutv brigade ke badhate dar ko rokane ke liye kadam uthaate to hinsa ko nishchit hi roka ja saktaa tha
 But he not only allowed the hooligans to rise and encouraged them to gain political power, but also helped to remove their fear of law from their mindless action
 ab bhi agar mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv, dm or zila police adhikari ek saath khadey ho jaaen to is ghaatak raajnneetik agenda kaa pardaafaash kiya ja saktaa he, iske masterminds ko pahachaanaa ja saktaa he or hinsa karne waalon ko kathghare main khadaa kiya ja saktaa he
 These officers have the opportunity to fulfill the oath of the Constitution and fulfill the expectations that citizens have from higher civil services
 tippaniyan The letter calls for the Prime Minister to write that our Prime Minister, who does not get tired in his election campaigns saying that the Constitution of India is the only book he worships, is also silent in this matter while his elected Chief Minister Playing with the same constitution
 ye saafe he ki sangh parivaar ke liye sanvaidhanik naitikta kaa koi mulya nahin he or wo bahusnkhyakon ke dabadabe ke vichaar ko maanata he
 This is a very serious time and we cannot just leave it like that
 ham sabhi nagarikon se nafrat or bantwaare kii is raajnneeti ke kilaaf ek hone kii maang karte hai
 We demand that the Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh resign for failing to abide by the Constitution he has sworn to implement
 ham jaanate hai ki ye tabhi ho paaegaa jab ham milakar janabhaawanaaon ko ubhaaren or unhen apane kaam ke liye zimmedaari kaa ahsaas karaate hue istife ke liye majaboor karen
 We would like to remind the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary and all members of the higher civil services that it is their constitutional obligation to establish the rule of law without fear, instead of perverse orders of their political masters
 isi ke saath elahabaad hycourt se aagrah kiya gaya he ki vah is ghatana kaa swat: sangyaan yani suo motu cognizance len or apni nigaraanee main ek nyaayik jaanch kaa aadesh den

 is patr main mukhyamantri aditya nath kii aalochana kii gai he, un par dharmandhta kaa paksh lene kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he or istife kii maang kii gai he
 These officers have written that they are not from any political party
 samvidhan ke mulyon ke alaava kisi or vichaardhaara main yakeen nahin rakhte
 i want to read some part of this letter for you - On December 3, 2018, mob violence was carried out in Bulandshahr, Uttar Pradesh with malice
 isamen bheed ko shant karne kii koshish kar rahe upi police ke ek bahadur afasar kii nrushans hatya kar di gai
 This became the most terrible turn in the direction of hate politics
 ye dikhaata he ki desh ke sabase aabaadi vaale rajya uttarapradesh main shashan ke moulik siddhanton, sanvaidhanik naitikta or maanviya saamaajik vyavhaar ko taak par rakh diya gaya he
 The chief minister of the state is promoting the domination of fundamentalism and majoritarianism
 ye ek aisa agenda he jo duusari har chiz par haaavee he
 According to the letter such incidents have happened in Uttar Pradesh before but till now we believed that whenever a political party forms a government, it rules with responsibility keeping aside the partisan political agenda to increase its political acceptability
 lekin bulandshahr kii ghatana se pehle upi main muslim samudaay ko daraane or alag-thalag karne kii lagaataar koshishen hoti rahi hai
 With Yogi Adityanath as the Chief Minister, our faith has been proved wrong and hooliganism and cheating have joined the mainstream of governance to not only intimidate the minorities but to teach a lesson to every person, police and administration who along with the minority community Dare to behave equally
 jab tak inspector subodh kumaar singh kii hatya ke maamle main jaanch puri nahin ho jaati tab tak kisi nattejey par pahunchnaa jaldbaazi hogi lekin isamen koi shaq nahin he ki jis tarah unki hatya hui usamen kuch bhi swaabhaavik yaa swat: sfoort nahin tha
 There is also no doubt about which political elements encouraged and instigated the violence
 jaanboojhkar bahusnkhyakon kii taaqat ko dikhaane kii koshish hui taaki ilaake main rahane vaale muslim samudaayon ko sandesh diya ja sake ki unhen dar main rahanaa hoga, wo bahusankhyak samudaay ke saanskrithik farmaanon ko maane or khud ko unase kamatar maane
 It is also written in the letter that the police and civil administration have succumbed to the distorted political system
 wo samvidhan ke prati apni praathmik vafadaari or kaanoon ke raaj ko bhul chuke hai jabaki unka sanvaidhanik darja unhen abhootpurv taaqat detaa he
 If they had taken steps to curb the growing fear of the Hindutva brigade, the violence could have been definitely prevented
 lekin unhone naa sirf gundgardee karne waalon ke hausale ko badhane diya or unhen raajnneetik taaqat hasil karne diya balki apni lachar karrwai se unke man se kaanoon ke dar ko hataane main bhi madad kii
 Even now, if the Chief Secretary, DGP, Home Secretary, DM and district police officers stand together, this deadly political agenda can be exposed, its masterminds can be identified and the perpetrators of violence should be put in the dock Can
 in adhikariyon ke saamne samvidhan kii shapath ko puraa karne kaa mauka he or ucch naagarik sevaaon se nagarikon ko jo ummiden hai unhen puraa karne kaa avasar he
 The comments khat main pradhanmantri kaa aahvaan karte hue likhaa gaya he ki hamaare pradhanmantri jo apane chunavi abhiyaanon main ye kehete nahin thakte ki bharat kaa samvidhan hi ekmaatr kitaab he jisaki wo puja karte hai, wo bhi is maamle main chuppi saadhe hue hai jabaki unke chune hue mukhyamantri usee samvidhan ke saath khilwaad kar rahe hai
 It is clear that constitutional morality has no value for the Sangh Parivar and it considers the idea of majority domination
 ye ek bahut hi gambhir samay he or ham ise yon hi nahin chhod sakate
 We demand all citizens to unite against this politics of hate and division
 ham maang karte hai ki uttarapradesh ke mukhyamantri samvidhan ke paalan main naakaam rahane ke liye istifa den jis samvidhan ko lagu karne kii unhone shapath khai he
 We know that this will happen only when we together raise public sentiments and force them to resign, making them feel responsible for their work
 ham mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv or ucch naagarik sevaaon ke sabhi sadasyon ko yaad dilaanaa chaahate hai ki ye unka sanvaidhanik daayitv he ki wo apane raajnneetik aakaaon ke vikrut adeshon ke bajaay bina dare kaanoon kaa raaj sthapit karen
 Simultaneously, the Allahabad High Court has been requested to take suo motu cognizance of this incident and order a judicial inquiry under its supervision
 insaaf kii bhi apni raajnneeti he
 Debaters argue on behalf of Hindus, argue on behalf of Muslims
 lekin jo peedit hota he uske kaam koi dharm nahin aata he
 Neither Islam nor Hindu
 wo akelaa ladata hua chand logon ke bharose ke sahare jeeta he
 Sob isliye insaaf ke liye jashn manaane waalon ko ek baar jagadish cor se poochna chahie ki 34 saal sangharsh unhone kiya yaa tivi main aane vaale pravaktaaon ne kiya
 Rather, if they do not meet, they should ask Mohsin's mother Shabana Sadiq Sheikh, if they cannot find it, then they should ask Rajni ji, wife of Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh, who was killed in Bulandshahr
 shabana or rajani kii ladaai bhi zakiya jaafaree or jagadish cor kii tarah akele kii ladaai he
 You must remember that picture of the crowd, the mob gathered in the name of the cow killed Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh
 16-17 din ho gaye mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 Meanwhile, the main accused also released a statement through whatsapp which went on TV
 is cese main police ke varisht adhikariyon kaa tabadalaa ho gaya lekin mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya
 The Chief Minister had also called a meeting after the incident about which there was no mention of Subodh Kumar Singh when the press release was issued, that strict action should be taken against those who killed cow
 baad main mukhyamantri adityanath ne peedit parivaar ko lakhanu bulaayaa, subodh kumaar singh kii patni rajani, unke bete unase milane gaye lekin abhi tak mukhya aaropee nahin pakadaa gaya he
 Today, more than 80 retired officials have written an open letter regarding the murder of Subodh Kumar Singh
 inamen iesces, iees or ipies, van seva or rajasav seva ke adhikari hai
 Some have been ambassadors in many important countries
 is suchi main purv rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar shiv shankar menon bhi hai
 The letter criticizes Chief Minister Aditya Nath, accusing him of favoring bigotry and demanding his resignation
 in afasaron ne likhaa he ki ve kisi raajnneetik dal se nahin hai
 Do not believe in any ideology other than the values of the constitution
 is patr kaa kuch hissaa aapke liye padhanaa chahta hum- 3 disambar, 2018 ko uttarapradesh ke bulandshahr main durbhaavna ke saath bheed kii hinsa ko anjaam diya gaya
 In this, a brave officer of the UP police, who was trying to calm the crowd, was brutally murdered
 ye nafrat kii raajnneeti kii disha main sabase bhayanak mode ban gaya
 It shows that Uttar Pradesh, the most populous state in the country, has kept the fundamental principles of governance, constitutional ethics and human social behavior at bay
 rajya ke mukhyamantri kattarta or bahusankhyakwaad ke varchasv ko badhaava de rahe hai
 This is an agenda that dominates everything else
 khat ke mutabik aisi ghatnaayen uttarapradesh main pehle bhi hui hai lekin abhi tak hamen vishwaas tha ki jab bhi koi raajnneetik dal sarkaar banaata he to wo pakshpaat bhare raajnneetik agenda ko alag rakhkar zimmedaari ke saath shashan karata he taaki uski raajnneetik sweekaaryata bade
 But before the Bulandshahr incident, there have been constant attempts to intimidate and isolate the Muslim community in UP
 yogi adityanath ke mukhyamantri rahete hamaara wo vishwaas galat sabit hua he or gundgardee or thagi shashan kii mukhyadhara main shaamil ho gaye hai taaki na sirf alpsankhyakon ko daraaya ja sake balki har us vyakti, police or prashasan ko sabak sikhaaya ja sake jo alpsankhyak samudaay ke saath barabari kaa vyavhaar karne kii himmat kare
 Until the investigation into the murder of Inspector Subodh Kumar Singh is complete, it is too early to come to any conclusion, but there is no doubt that nothing was natural or spontaneous in the manner in which he was killed
 is baat main bhi koi shaq nahin he ki kin raajnneetik tatwon ne hinsa ko badhaava or uksaava diya
 There was a deliberate attempt to show the strength of the majority in order to give a message to the Muslim communities living in the area that they have to live in fear, accept the cultural decrees of the majority community and consider themselves inferior to them
 khat main ye bhi likhaa gaya he ki police or naagarik prashasan vikrut raajnneetik tantra ke aage jhuk chukaa he
 They have forgotten their primary loyalty to the Constitution and the rule of law, while their constitutional status gives them unprecedented power
 agar wo hindutv brigade ke badhate dar ko rokane ke liye kadam uthaate to hinsa ko nishchit hi roka ja saktaa tha
 But he not only allowed the hooligans to rise and encouraged them to gain political power, but also helped to remove their fear of law from their mindless action
 ab bhi agar mukhya sachiv, dijipi, grih sachiv, dm or zila police adhikari ek saath khadey ho jaaen to is ghaatak raajnneetik agenda kaa pardaafaash kiya ja saktaa he, iske masterminds ko pahachaanaa ja saktaa he or hinsa karne waalon ko kathghare main khadaa kiya ja saktaa he
 These officers have the opportunity to fulfill the oath of the Constitution and fulfill the expectations that citizens have from higher civil services
 tippaniyan The letter calls for the Prime Minister to write that our Prime Minister, who does not get tired in his election campaigns saying that the Constitution of India is the only book he worships, is also silent in this matter while his elected Chief Minister Playing with the same constitution
 ye saafe he ki sangh parivaar ke liye sanvaidhanik naitikta kaa koi mulya nahin he or wo bahusnkhyakon ke dabadabe ke vichaar ko maanata he
 This is a very serious time and we cannot just leave it like that
